subject_type_icon = {
	type = country
	log_loc_errors = no

	text = {
		trigger = {
			is_subject_type = subject_type_customs_union
		}

	}

            is_subject_type = subject_type_protectorate

pound_currency_accumulation = {
	type = country
	log_loc_errors = no

	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				var:stockpiling_pound_sterling_c_var_2 > 0
				var:stockpiling_irish_pound_c_var_2 > 0
				var:stockpiling_egyptian_pound_c_var_2 > 0
			}
		}

		localization_key = green_arow_bellow
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				var:stockpiling_pound_sterling_c_var_2 < 0
				var:stockpiling_irish_pound_c_var_2 < 0
				var:stockpiling_egyptian_pound_c_var_2 < 0
			}
		}
		localization_key = red_arow
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				var:stockpiling_pound_sterling_c_var_2 = 0
				var:stockpiling_irish_pound_c_var_2 = 0
				var:stockpiling_egyptian_pound_c_var_2 = 0
			}
		}
		localization_key = yellow_arrow
	}
}

law_monetary_policy	= {
	type = country
	log_loc_errors = no

	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_law = law_type:law_no_monetary_policy
		}

		localization_key = law_no_monetary_policy
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_law = law_type:law_war_economy
		}

		localization_key = law_war_economy
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			var:revaluation_on = 1
		}

		localization_key = law_revaluation_100

	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_revaluation_25
			}
		}

		localization_key = law_revaluation_25

	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_revaluation_50
			}
		}

		localization_key = law_revaluation_50

	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_revaluation_75
			}
		}

		localization_key = law_revaluation_75

	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_revaluation_100
			}
		}

		localization_key = law_revaluation_100

	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_devaluation_25
			}
		}

		localization_key = law_devaluation_25

	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_devaluation_50
			}
		}

		localization_key = law_devaluation_50

	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_devaluation_75
			}
		}

		localization_key = law_devaluation_75

	}
  
	text = {
		trigger = {
			var:devaluation_on = 1
		}

		localization_key = law_devaluation_100

	}
}
law_monetary_policy_texture	= {
	type = country
	log_loc_errors = no

	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_law = law_type:law_no_monetary_policy
		}

		localization_key = law_no_monetary_policy_texture
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_law = law_type:law_war_economy
		}

		localization_key = law_war_economy_texture
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_revaluation_25
				has_law = law_type:law_revaluation_50
				has_law = law_type:law_revaluation_75
				has_law = law_type:law_revaluation_100
				var:revaluation_on = 1
			}
		}

		localization_key = law_revaluation_texture

	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_devaluation_25
				has_law = law_type:law_devaluation_50
				has_law = law_type:law_devaluation_75
				has_law = law_type:law_devaluation_100
				var:devaluation_on = 1
			}
		}

		localization_key = law_devaluation_texture
	}
}

player_help = {
	type = country
	log_loc_errors = no

	text = {
		trigger = {
			var:player_help = 1
			var:player_help_reverce = 1
		}

		localization_key = off
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			var:player_help = 0
			var:player_help_reverce = 0
		}

		localization_key = on
	}
}
